While neural methods have shown promising results under moderately sparse observations, their inference efficiency at high resolutions is limited, and their accuracy degrades substantially in the extremely sparse regime. In this work, we propose the Di-BiLPS, a unified neural framework that effectively handle both forward and inverse PDE problems under extremely sparse observations. Di-BiLPS combines a variational autoencoder to compress high-dimensional inputs into a compact latent space, a latent diffusion module to model uncertainty, and contrastive learning to align representations. Operating entirely in this latent space, the framework achieves efficient inference while retaining flexible input-output mapping. In addition, we introduce a PDE-informed denoising algorithm based on a variance-preserving diffusion process, which further improves inference efficiency. Extensive experiments on multiple PDE benchmarks demonstrate that Di-BiLPS consistently achieves SOTA performance under extremely sparse inputs (as low as 3%), while substantially reducing computational cost. Moreover, Di-BiLPS enables zero-shot super-resolution, as it allows predictions over continuous spatial-temporal domains.

### [433] [Provable Quantization with Randomized Hadamard Transform](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13810)
*Ying Feng,Piotr Indyk,Michael Kapralov,Dmitry Krachun,Boris Prokhorov*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文研究了随机投影后进行标量量化的基础方法，提出了一种使用单一随机化Hadamard变换的抖动量化变体。该方法在应用Hadamard变换后减去随机标量偏移再进行量化，以极低成本注入额外随机性。作者证明了该方法无偏，且均方误差界渐近匹配真实随机旋转矩阵的性能。特别地，他们证明了抖动版TurboQuant在每坐标b比特时均方误差达到(π√3/2 + o(1))·4^{-b}，其中o(1)项在所有单位向量和所有维度上随量化级数增加而一致消失。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的向量量化方法中，稠密随机旋转虽有理论保证但计算复杂度高(Θ(d²))，而随机化Hadamard变换虽将代价降至O(d log d)，但其离散结构导致分析复杂且只能提供较弱或纯经验的压缩保证。本文旨在设计一种兼具高效计算与强理论保证的量化方法。

Method: 提出抖动量化与单一随机化Hadamard变换结合的方法：首先对输入向量应用Hadamard变换HD，然后减去随机标量偏移再进行量化。通过这种"抖动"(dithering)技术以极低成本注入额外随机性，弥补Hadamard变换离散结构带来的随机性不足。

Result: 证明了该方法无偏，且均方误差界渐近匹配真实随机旋转矩阵的性能。具体地，抖动版TurboQuant在每坐标b比特量化下达到(π√3/2 + o(1))·4^{-b}的均方误差，其中o(1)项在所有单位向量和所有维度上随量化级数增加而一致消失。

Conclusion: 本文成功结合了Hadamard变换的计算效率与抖动技术的理论保证，提供了一种既高效又具有强理论保证的向量量化方案，适用于相似性搜索、联邦学习、KV缓存压缩等机器学习应用场景。

Abstract: Vector quantization via random projection followed by scalar quantization is a fundamental primitive in machine learning, with applications ranging from similarity search to federated learning and KV cache compression. While dense random rotations yield clean theoretical guarantees, they require $Θ(d^2)$ time. The randomized Hadamard transform $HD$ reduces this cost to $O(d \log d)$, but its discrete structure complicates analysis and leads to weaker or purely empirical compression guarantees.
  In this work, we study a variant of this approach: dithered quantization with a single randomized Hadamard transform. Specifically, the quantizer applies $HD$ to the input vector and subtracts a random scalar offset before quantizing, injecting additional randomness at negligible cost. We prove that this approach is unbiased and provides mean squared error bounds that asymptotically match those achievable with truly random rotation matrices. In particular, we prove that a dithered version of TurboQuant achieves mean squared error $\bigl(π\sqrt{3}/2 + o(1)\bigr) \cdot 4^{-b}$ at $b$ bits per coordinate, where the $o(1)$ term vanishes uniformly over all unit vectors and all dimensions as the number of quantization levels grows.

</details>

Both pipelines use Transformer encoders and output a daily anomaly score, derived from predictive uncertainty estimated via an ensemble of multilayer perceptrons to improve robustness to real-world wearable variability. While each framework independently demonstrates strong predictive power, we show that they capture complementary physiological signatures. Consequently, we propose a late-fusion strategy that synergistically combines the anomaly signals from both architectures into a unified decision score. We benchmark our methodology on the 2nd e-Prevention Grand Challenge dataset, where our fused model achieves a 8% relative improvement over the competition-winning baseline. Our results, supported by extensive ablation studies, suggest that the integration of diverse digital phenotypes, cardiac, motion, and sleep, is essential for the high-fidelity detection of psychotic relapse in real-world settings.

### [435] [Reducing cross-sample prediction churn in scientific machine learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13826)
*Gordan Prastalo,Kevin Maik Jablonka*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 论文发现科学机器学习模型在重采样训练数据时预测结果存在显著差异（cross-sample prediction churn，即交叉样本预测波动），标准参数侧技术无法解决，而数据侧方法（K-自助采样集成和提出的twin-bootstrap）能有效降低这一差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学机器学习只报告预测性能，但不报告同一预测在不同训练数据采样下是否稳定，缺乏对预测可靠性的评估。

Method: 提出cross-sample prediction churn概念衡量预测波动性；对比参数侧（deep ensembles, MC dropout, SWA）和数据侧（K-bootstrap bagging, twin-bootstrap）方法。Twin-bootstrap通过两个网络在独立自助样本上联合训练并加入sym-KL一致性损失来减少波动。

Result: 在9个化学基准上，两次训练在准确率上仅差1.3-4.2个百分点，但对8.0-21.8%的分子分类标签不一致。参数侧技术无效；K-bootstrap bagging降低波动40-54%不损失准确率；twin-bootstrap在2倍计算成本下比bagging-K=2再中位降低45%的波动。

Conclusion: 交叉样本预测波动应作为科学机器学习基准报告的重要指标，与预测性能并列，因为参数侧和数据侧方法在该指标上才有本质区别。

Abstract: Scientific machine learning reports predictive performance. It does not report whether the same prediction would survive a different draw of training data. Across $9$ chemistry benchmarks, two classifiers trained on independent bootstraps of the same training set agree on aggregate accuracy to within $1.3\text{--}4.2$ percentage points but disagree on the class label of $8.0\text{--}21.8\%$ of test molecules. We call this gap \emph{cross-sample prediction churn}. The standard parameter-side techniques (deep ensembles, MC dropout, stochastic weight averaging) do not reduce this gap; two data-side methods do. The first is $K$-bootstrap bagging, which cuts the rate $40\text{--}54\%$ on every dataset at no accuracy cost ($K{\times}$-ERM compute). The second is \emph{twin-bootstrap}, our proposal: two networks trained jointly on independent bootstraps with a sym-KL consistency loss between their predictions, which at matched $2{\times}$-ERM compute reduces churn a further median $45\%$ beyond bagging-$K{=}2$. Cross-sample prediction churn deserves a column alongside predictive performance in scientific-ML benchmark reports, because without it the parameter-side and data-side methods are indistinguishable on the metric they actually differ on.

</details>


### [436] [Topology-Preserving Neural Operator Learning via Hodge Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13834)
*Dongzhe Zheng,Tao Zhong,Christine Allen-Blanchette*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Hodge Spectral Duality (HSD)框架，基于Hodge理论和算子分裂，将物理场方程解算子分解为拓扑（可学习）和几何（不可学习）两部分，实现结构保持的混合欧拉-拉格朗日网络架构，在几何网格上取得优异精度与效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经网络在几何网格上求解物理场方程时，频谱干扰严重，拓扑自由度（不可学习）与几何动力学（可学习）纠缠不清，导致模型难以同时保证精度和物理守恒律。

Method: 1) 从函数空间视角揭示Hodge正交性可分离拓扑与几何成分；2) 基于Hodge理论和算子分裂推导算子级分解；3) 提出Hybrid Eulerian-Lagrangian架构，利用离散微分形式捕获拓扑主导成分，用正交辅助环境空间表示局部动力学；4) 引入代数级归纳偏置Hodge Spectral Duality (HSD)。

Result: 在几何网格上达到更优的精度和效率，且对物理不变量具有更强的保真度。

Conclusion: HSD框架有效解决了几何网格上物理场学习的频谱干扰问题，为结构保持的物理信息神经网络提供了新范式。

Abstract: In this paper, we study solution operators of physical field equations on geometric meshes from a function-space perspective. We reveal that Hodge orthogonality fundamentally resolves spectral interference by isolating unlearnable topological degrees of freedom from learnable geometric dynamics, enabling an additive approximation confined to structure-preserving subspaces. Building on Hodge theory and operator splitting, we derive a principled operator-level decomposition. The result is a Hybrid Eulerian-Lagrangian architecture with an algebraic-level inductive bias we call Hodge Spectral Duality (HSD). In our framework, we use discrete differential forms to capture topology-dominated components and an orthogonal auxiliary ambient space to represent complex local dynamics. Our method achieves superior accuracy and efficiency on geometric graphs with enhanced fidelity to physical invariants. Our code is available at https://github.com/ContinuumCoder/Hodge-Spectral-Duality

</details>

By providing a structured, synthetic ground truth, this work establishes a foundational benchmark for trustworthy AI in aquatics. The outcomes of this research promise to enhance the reliability of automated coaching and open a plethora of future directions in "Meta-Agent" development and athletic profiling, ultimately bridging the gap between raw data engineering and practical sports science application.

### [439] [Mechanism Plausibility in Generative Agent-Based Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12824)
*Patrick Zhao,David Huu Pham,Nicholas Vincent*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 这篇论文提出了“机制合理性量表”（Mechanism Plausibility Scale），用于评估LLM-ABM（基于大语言模型的智能体模型）在社会模拟中是否具备解释力，而不仅仅是生成或预测能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM-ABM的研究多集中于测试模型能否生成多样现象（如人类行为、博弈情境），但忽视了能力（capability）、预测（prediction）与解释（explanation）之间的根本区别。研究者认为，真正的解释需要揭示现象是如何通过相关组织的实体与活动产生的，而这在现有评估中往往被忽略。

Method: 整合近期LLM-ABM研究与当代科学哲学文献，操作化定义了一个四层次的“机制合理性量表”。该量表将模型的生成充分性（能否复现现象）与机制合理性（现象如何产生）分开评估，并明确了预测性模型与解释性模型的不同角色。

Result: 构建了一个四层量表，用于区分模型在生成现象和解释现象方面的贡献，帮助建模者判断模拟实验在能力提升还是解释进步上的定位。

Conclusion: 通过引入“机制合理性量表”，该研究为LLM-ABM社区提供了一个清晰的评估框架，能够更好地区分预测性模拟与解释性模拟，推进社会模拟在科学解释层面的可信度与实用性。

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) can generate high-level diverse phenomena without explicitly programmed rules. This capability has led to their adoption within different agent-based models (ABMs) and social simulations. Recently, research has aim to test whether they are capable of generating different phenomena of interest, for example, human behavior on social media platforms or performance in game-theoretic scenarios.
  However, capability, prediction, and explanation are different -- drawing from the philosophy of science and mechanisms literature, \textit{explanation} requires showing, to some degree, how a phenomenon is produced by related organized entities and activities. For modelers, describing the characteristics of an experiment or whether a simulation provides progress in capability (or explanation), can be difficult without being grounded in potentially distant research areas.
  We integrate recent work on LLM-ABMs with contemporary philosophy of science literature and use it to operationalize a definition of `plausibility' in a four-level scale. Our scale separates the evaluation of a model's generative sufficiency (ability to reproduce a phenomenon) from its mechanistic plausibility (how the phenomenon could be produced), and clarifies the distinct roles of different models, such as predictive and explanatory ones. We introduce this as the Mechanism Plausibility Scale.

</details>


### [440] [ChipMATE: Multi-Agent Training via Reinforcement Learning for Enhanced RTL Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12857)
*Zhongkai Yu,Yichen Lin,Chenyang Zhou,Yuwei Zhang,Kun Zhou,Junxia Cui,Haotian Ye,Zhengding Hu,Zaifeng Pan,Ruiyi Wang,Yujie Zhao,Hejia Zhang,Jingbo Shang,Jishen Zhao,Yufei Ding*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: ChipMATE 是首个自训练的多智能体框架，通过 Verilog 智能体与 Python 参考模型智能体相互验证，解决了现有 API 式 RTL 代码生成系统与实际工业流程不匹配的问题，无需黄金测试基准即可实现高准确率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 API 式 RTL 生成系统与实际工业实践存在根本性不一致：（1）假设生成时已有黄金测试基准；（2）依赖闭源 API，无法满足芯片厂商的隔离安全要求；（3）无法在厂商的专有 RTL 代码库上训练，宝贵的内部数据无法使用。自训练模型虽解决了部署约束，但仍限于单轮生成，忽视了验证在工业流程中的关键作用。

Method: 提出 ChipMATE 框架：（1）双智能体架构：Verilog 智能体 + Python 参考模型智能体，两者相互验证输出，无需黄金标准；（2）基于回溯的推理流程，防止错误在多轮交互中传播；（3）两阶段训练流程：先单独训练每个智能体以饱和其代码生成能力，再联合训练团队以有效协作；（4）混合数据生成框架，产出 64.4K 高质量参考模型训练样本。

Result: 使用 4B 和 9B 基础模型，ChipMATE 在 VerilogEval V2 上分别达到 75.0% 和 80.1% 的 pass@1，超越了所有现有的自训练模型，甚至超过了 1600B 参数的 DeepSeek V4。

Conclusion: 通过多智能体相互验证的设计，ChipMATE 成功将工业实践中"交叉比对"的验证范式引入自训练模型，既满足部署安全需求，又在无需黄金测试基准的情况下达到了超越超大模型的性能。代码和模型权重已开源。

Abstract: Existing API-based agentic systems for RTL code generation are fundamentally misaligned with industrial practice: they assume a golden testbench is available at generation time, rely on closed-source APIs incompatible with chip vendors' air-gapped security requirements, and cannot be trained on vendors' proprietary RTL codebases, leaving valuable internal data unused. Recent self-trained models address the deployment constraint but remain single-turn generators that overlook the critical role of verification in real industrial flows.
  To bridge these gaps, we present ChipMATE, the first self-trained multi-agent framework for RTL generation. Inspired by industrial practice where correctness emerges from cross-comparison between independently written RTL modules and reference models, ChipMATE pairs a Verilog agent with a Python reference-model agent that mutually verify each other's outputs without any golden oracle. We design a backtrack-based inference workflow to prevent error propagation across turns, and a two-stage training pipeline that first trains each agent individually to saturate its code-generation capability, then trains the team jointly to collaborate effectively. To support the training, we further build a hybrid data-generation framework that produces 64.4K high-quality reference model training samples. ChipMATE achieves 75.0\% and 80.1\% pass@1 on VerilogEval V2 with 4B and 9B base models, outperforming all existing self-trained models and even DeepSeek V4 with 1600B parameters. Our code and model weights are publicly available in https://github.com/zhongkaiyu/ChipMATE.

</details>

### [442] [Embodied Multi-Agent Coordination by Aligning World Models Through Dialogue](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.12920)
*Vardhan Dongre,Dilek Hakkani-Tür*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文研究基于LLM的具身智能体在部分可观测环境下是否真正具备通过对话进行沟通的能力。作者扩展了PARTNR基准，引入自然语言对话通道，并提出了世界模型对齐的评估框架（观测收敛性、信息新颖性、信念敏感通信）。实验表明，对话能显著减少行动冲突（40-83个百分点），但反而降低了任务成功率，揭示了当前模型在"表面协调"与"真正世界模型对齐"之间存在差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有具身智能体协作研究多假设智能体可以完全观测环境或通过隐式方式协调，但部分可观测环境下的协作若无通信在理论上是困难的。虽然通信在原则上可以弥合观测差距、对齐世界模型，但当前LLM驱动的智能体是否真正具备这种沟通能力尚不清楚。本文旨在检验LLM智能体是否真的能通过对话实现世界模型对齐，而非仅仅是表面上的协调。

Method: 1) 扩展PARTNR基准，为两个部分可观测的具身智能体添加自然语言对话通道，使其在任务执行过程中可通信。2) 提出世界模型对齐评估框架，包含三个指标：观测收敛性（私有世界模型是否随时间对齐）、信息新颖性（消息是否传递了对方缺乏的信息）、信念敏感通信（智能体是否建模对方的认知状态）。3) 在三种LLM上进行实验对比。

Result: 1) 对话使行动冲突减少40-83个百分点。2) 但任务成功率反而低于无通信的静默协调基线。3) 通过提出的三个指标，揭示了表面协调与真正世界模型对齐之间的差距。

Conclusion: 当前LLM驱动的具身智能体虽然能通过对话减少行动冲突，但并未实现真正的世界模型对齐，甚至损害了任务完成效率。本文提出的评估框架有效刻画了这一差距，为未来提升智能体深层沟通能力指明了方向。

Abstract: Effective collaboration between embodied agents requires more than acting in a shared environment; it demands communication grounded in each agent's evolving understanding of the world. When agents can only partially observe their surroundings, coordination without communication is provably hard, but communication can, in principle, bridge this gap by allowing agents to share observations and align their world models. In this work, we examine whether LLM-based embodied agents actually realize the ability to communicate. We extend PARTNR, a benchmark for collaborative household robotics, with a natural-language dialogue channel that enables two agents with partial observability to communicate during task execution. To evaluate whether dialogue leads to genuine world-model alignment rather than superficial coordination, we propose a framework for measuring world-model alignment defined over per-agent world graphs: observation convergence (do private world models align over time?), information novelty (do messages convey what the partner lacks?), and belief-sensitive messaging (do agents model what their partner knows?). Our experiments across three LLMs reveal that dialogue reduces action conflicts 40 to 83 percentage points but degrades task success relative to silent coordination. Using our metrics, we characterize the gap between superficial coordination and genuine world-model alignment, and identify where current models fall on this spectrum.

### [443] [Conveyor Parcel Routing with Order-Contiguous Arrivals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13035)
*Takuro Kato,Keisuke Okumura*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出在线多智能体路径规划中的订单连续性问题（online MAPF-OC），要求同一订单的包裹连续到达工作站以减少分拣成本，并提出了完整的多项式时间算法DOPP，通过三层结构（订单级序列搜索→智能体级优先级细化→优先级规划求解）高效生成高质量方案，在实际仓库布局验证中表现出可扩展性和时效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在仓库物流中，包裹从自动存储系统出料口经传送网络路由到工作站，除了避免碰撞，实际运营还需要订单连续到达（同一订单的包裹在到达序列中连续出现），以减少下游重新分拣的工作量。现有方法未考虑这一关键约束。

Method: 提出DOPP（双顺序优先级规划）算法，采用三层结构：（i）搜索订单级别的到达序列；（ii）在订单内部细化智能体（包裹）级别的优先级；（iii）通过优先级规划综合出可行解。算法完整且多项式时间可解。

Result: 在多种传送网络布局（包括实际仓库布局）上的实验表明，DOPP在实际中具有良好的可扩展性，能够在紧张的时间预算内生成高质量的计划方案。

Conclusion: DOPP有效解决了带订单连续性约束的在线多智能体路径规划问题，为仓库物流中的订单连续到达需求提供了高效可行的求解框架。

Abstract: In warehouse logistics, parcels released from the outfeed of an automated storage system must be routed through conveyor networks to workstations. Beyond collision avoidance, practical operations impose an additional requirement of order-contiguous arrivals: at each delivery point, parcels belonging to the same order must arrive as a consecutive block in the arrival sequence to reduce downstream re-sorting effort. We formalize this problem as online multi-agent path finding with order-contiguity (online MAPF-OC), where agents (i.e., parcels) appear over time and exit upon delivery. To efficiently solve online MAPF-OC, we propose Dual-Ordering Prioritized Planning (DOPP), a complete polynomial-time algorithm with a three-level structure that (i) searches order-level arrival sequences, (ii) refines agent-level priorities, and (iii) synthesizes feasible solutions via prioritized planning. Experiments on various conveyor-network layouts, including those derived from actual warehouses, demonstrate DOPP's practical scalability and ability to generate high-quality plans within tight time budgets.

To allocate responsibility among agents, we utilise the Shapley value and formally show that this method satisfies key desirable properties, including fairness and consistency. ### [446] [When Does Hierarchy Help? Benchmarking Agent Coordination in Event-Driven Industrial Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13172)
*Ziqi Wang,Yuhao Yang,Zhiwei Ling,Wenzhuo Qian,Hailiang Zhao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准大多评估弱耦合环境中的任务完成度，缺乏对共享、动态演化系统中层次化与耦合约束下的协调机制研究，特别是不同协调范式何时成功或失败的问题尚未得到充分探索。

Method: 构建DESBench基准测试，基于共享离散事件驱动的工业调度环境，涵盖多时间尺度决策、部分可观测性和动态耦合约束。定义了评估有效性、约束对齐、协调效率和鲁棒性的指标，并研究了四种协调范式：集中式、层次式、异层次式和全息式。

Result: 集中式协调鲁棒且通信高效但扩展性差；层次式协调通过分解提升效率但存在跨层级偏差；异层次式协调灵活但通信开销大；全息式协调约束满足良好但全局鲁棒性下降。

Conclusion: 协调设计从根本上影响复杂环境中智能体系统的行为，揭示了仅靠结果指标无法捕捉的结构性权衡，强调了未来多智能体系统研究需要更自适应、有原则和动态的协调机制。

Abstract: Recent advances in agent and multi-agent systems have shown strong performance on tool use, reasoning, and collaborative tasks. However, existing benchmarks mostly evaluate task completion in weakly coupled environments, and provide limited support for studying coordination in shared, dynamically evolving systems with hierarchy and coupled constraints. This leaves an important question underexplored: when do different coordination paradigms succeed or fail? We introduce Distributed Event-driven Scheduling Benchmark (DESBench), a benchmark for evaluating agent coordination in hierarchical event-driven scheduling. Built on a shared discrete-event driven environment in industrial scheduling, our benchmark captures multi-timescale decision making, partial observability, and dynamically coupled constraints. We define tasks and metrics that evaluate effectiveness, constraint alignment, coordination efficiency, and robustness, and focus on four representative coordination paradigms: centralized, hierarchical, heterarchical, and holonic. These paradigms correspond to distinct mechanisms of information flow, decision authority, and conflict resolution. Our controlled evaluations reveal clear coordination trade-offs: centralized coordination is robust and communication-efficient but scales poorly with difficulty; hierarchical coordination improves efficiency through decomposition but suffers from cross-level misalignment; heterarchical coordination is flexible but communication-heavy; and holonic coordination satisfies constraints well but loses global robustness. These findings demonstrate that coordination design fundamentally shapes agent system behavior in complex environments, revealing structural trade-offs that cannot be captured by outcome metrics alone and underscoring the imperative for more adaptive, principled, and dynamic coordination mechanisms in future MAS research.

</details>


### [447] [Constitutional Governance in Metric Spaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13362)
*Ehud Shapiro,Nimrod Talmon*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出一个在度量空间中的宪政治理框架，将聚合、审议、修正和共识整合为单一多项式时间流程，支持数字社区和组织的民主治理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有计算社会选择和算法决策理论虽然提供丰富的聚合理论，但缺乏端到端的多项式时间流程来实现平等自治；关键度量空间聚合器是NP难的，且现有工作孤立地处理聚合、审议、修正和共识。

Method: 设计一个宪法框架，每个可修正组件指定度量空间、聚合规则和超级多数阈值。成员提交理想元素（投票+个人提案），任何成员可提交获得超级多数公开支持的公共提案。宪法规则评分提案与现状，采用正最大分数的提案；修正宪法需更高阈值。提出广义中位数作为工作规则。

Result: 建立框架级保证，证明无虚报弱占优诚实投票；研究妥协差距（最佳峰值与无约束最优之间的差距）——一维为零，一般有界，模拟中简单启发式可缩小差距。在七个经典设定上实例化框架。

Conclusion: 通过统一度量空间聚合、现实意识社会选择、超级多数修正、宪政共识、审议联盟形成和AI调解，为数字社区和组织的宪政民主治理提供了综合性解决方案。

Abstract: Computational social choice and algorithmic decision theory offer rich aggregation theory but no end-to-end, polynomial-time process for egalitarian self-governance: prior work treats aggregation, deliberation, amendment, and consensus in isolation, and key metric-space aggregators are NP-hard. We propose constitutional governance in metric spaces, integrating these stages into one polynomial-time process. The constitution assigns, per amendable component, a metric space, aggregation rule, and supermajority threshold. Each member submits an ideal element -- both vote and personal proposal. Any member may then submit a public proposal carrying supermajority public support under the revealed votes -- sourced from coalition deliberation, optimization, or AI mediation. The constitutional rule scores proposals against the status quo, adopting the supported proposal of positive maximal score (else retaining the status quo); the same rule, possibly with a higher threshold, amends the constitution itself. We develop the generalised median as the worked rule, establish framework-level guarantees, prove no misreport weakly dominates sincere voting, and study the compromise gap between best peak and unconstrained optimum -- zero in one dimension, bounded in general, narrowed in simulation by a simple heuristic. We instantiate the framework on seven canonical settings; the mean appears as a utilitarian alternative in the appendix. By unifying metric-space aggregation, reality-aware social choice, supermajority amendment, constitutional consensus, deliberative coalition formation, and AI mediation, this work delivers a comprehensive solution to the constitutional democratic governance of digital communities and organisations.

</details>


### [448] [EconAI: Dynamic Persona Evolution and Memory-Aware Agents in Evolving Economic Environments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.13762)
*Annie Liu,Zane Cao,Lang Chen,Zongxin Xu,Zigan Wang*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文提出EconAI框架，通过经济情绪指数(ESI)、记忆加权和动态决策机制，让LLM驱动的经济代理能同时进行短期优化和长期战略规划，首次在统一框架中模拟宏观/微观经济环境与交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的经济模拟框架无法捕捉短期优化与长期战略规划之间的相互作用，传统方法依赖静态数据驱动预测，缺乏对经济情绪、市场波动和个人目标的自适应行为。

Method: 提出EconAI框架，包含三个核心机制：经济情绪指数(ESI)量化经济信念、记忆加权调整历史数据的影响、动态决策机制连接工作-消费行为，使代理能根据市场信号和长期目标自适应调整决策。

Result: EconAI在经济响应稳定性、复现真实就业-消费周期以及决策鲁棒性方面均有显著提升。

Conclusion: EconAI是首个在统一框架中模拟宏观/微观经济环境与交互的LLM驱动模拟系统，是实现更真实、自适应经济代理模拟的关键进展。

Abstract: The integration of large language models (LLMs) in economic simulations has significantly enhanced agent-based modeling, yet existing frameworks struggle to capture the interplay between short-term optimization and long-term strategic planning. Conventional approaches rely on static data-driven predictions, failing to incorporate adaptive behaviors influenced by economic sentiment, market volatility, and individual goals. To address these limitations, we introduce a novel EconAI framework, incorporating economic sentiment indexing (ESI), memory weighting, and dynamic decision-making mechanisms. By quantifying economic belief, adjusting historical data influence, and linking work-consumption behaviors, EconAI achieves a more human-like decision process, where agents adapt their actions based on both market signals and long-term objectives. It is the first LLM-powered simulation system that can simulate the macro/microeconomic environment and interactions in a unified framework. Empirical evaluations show that EconAI improves stability in economic responses, better replicates real-world employment-consumption cycles, and enhances overall decision robustness. This advancement marks a crucial step towards more realistic, adaptive economic agent simulations.

</details>
